I am extremely frustrated with this dentist. I chose this dentist because they are contracted with my insurance. I was very clear from the beginning that I wanted to have my wisdom teeth checked out because I thought they needed to be extracted. It wasn't until the DDS (who was not Jeffrey A. Stratford-Jones DDS; I, in fact, never saw him during my three visits to the practice) came to examine me at the end of my first appointment that I found out that they don't actually extract teeth there! I would have chosen another dentist who could extract teeth. I felt like this behavior was extremely misleading and was purposeful so they could perform procedures and collect fees without actually addressing the root cause of my issues. Furthermore, during my third appointment, the DDS and assistant were talking about a patient they had referred for extraction and the DDS caused the tooth to break apart causing the patient extreme pain. Why would I see a dentist they recommend after that story?! My first appointment for cleaning was also miserable. The hygienist was extremely rude. She told me that I would have to get braces and, even after telling her multiple times that I would not get braces, she kept insisting that was the only treatment plan. She also kept telling me that I had gum loss and was making it seem like my teeth were falling out. Only later did she mention that my gums were actually within normal range. I had to request that she would not treat me during my second and third appointments. My second and third appointments were fine and I appreciate being checked in on after the procedures. My real frustration comes from their billing practices and the rudeness of the Office Manager Krista. The first EOB I received for cleaning said that I owed almost $200. After emailing Krista she told me that they write off those charges. I should have been informed that was the case before I received an EOB. Krista did let me know that each of the two subsequent procedures I needed would cost $156. I was not informed that some charges wouldn't be sent to my insurance so the EOB would say I only owed $46 when in reality I actually did owe $156 per procedure. I emailed Krista and she said that I would get a refund after my insurance paid. After I emailed again she said there would be no refund. She then became extremely rude and said that I signed the treatment plan so I should have known that they wouldn't even bother to bill my insurance for some charges. I would be less upset if she hadn't been so rude in recent emails and if she had actually explained all of the charges to me. I will never go back to this dentist.</text>

<resp>None</resp><Time>1602460666118</Time>< Review>
It is with a heavy heart I give Rip Current a 3 star. The beer is 5 stars all day long, but the brewery has not adapted well to the Covid restrictions. Food is required to drink on site and instead of getting a food truck like most other breweries your only option is a slice of pizza, either pepperoni or cheese. The pizza was horrible, the crust was like cardboard. I should have just thrown my money in the garbage. 1 star for the pizza, 5 stars for the beer. If you are visiting during the covid restrictions just be prepared to pay a premium fee and toss the pizza out. When the covid restrictions lift or when they get an actual food truck the rating will be 5 stars for sure.</Review>

< text>
Great local spot, very friendly relaxed atmosphere. Truly decent beer.
Edit I did rate this place five stars but now I can only give it two. Starting near the beginning of 2020 there was a noticeable change in the flavor and quality of beer. The two things I ask myself when I am at a brewery are: 1 would I like to drink this beer? And 2 would I like to drink this beer here. Unfortunately my answer to both is, no. I used to be greeted with a smile but those days are far gone. I walked into the San Marcos location the other day and there was a kid behind the bar on his phone. He half looked up at me then went back to his phone. He acted entitled like he was the owners son or a brewer who's job wasn't dealing with customers or something. I stood at the bar for a while looking for some eye contact but no one appeared. I just walked out without ordering. I still stop in every now and then after work but the beer is so bad. Lupulin Lust was the only solid beer and it now tastes so bad I do not enjoy drinking it. I have tried to power it down but it is work now. Low quality beer, low quality employees. Do not go here.<//text>

<GmapID>0x80dc75419f6a3a31:0x89e3538cfbc8937e< /GmapID>< review>
I came on a Saturday around 5pm in a group of 4. We had no problem finding a table at that time. Nice selection! The 4 of us with varying tastes were all able to find at least a couple beers we liked.

Favorite Beers:
- Java Storm: My favorite! Now in my top 3 for dark beers. If you like stouts/porters with a strong coffee profile you will love this. It wasn't as bitter as I expected with it having "Imperial" in the name.
- Take Off Triple: I normally don't like triples, but this was excellent.
- SD-Style Hefeweizen: Very nice! Fruity.< /review>

<Text>A visit to a body shop, any body shop, is probably not going to be the most pleasant of experiences.  Visiting a shop most likely means your vehicle was involved in accident, and something like this is certainly not going to put you in the best of moods.

However, Danny and Jose and his team at Big Rig Collision helped to make the entire "ordeal" as easy and as painless as possible for me.

I initially showed without an appointment.  I showed up because I wanted to MAKE an appointment, for an estimate.  Danny was able to give me an estimate on the spot.  While I was there, he gave me a small tour, which included pointing out his 70-year-old father who was working in the shop at the time!  Danny, literally, "grew up" around cars and body shops!

From what I've since learned, matching a vehicle's color is not an exact science.  It's not as if you can pick out that exact color from the paint store down the street.  Instead, matching a color involves starting with a similar base and mixing colors until you have a match.

This was Number One on my small list of worries.  It turns out I was worried for nothing.  Danny and his team were able to match the color PERFECTLY.  They did a GREAT JOB with my car!  There is no sign it was ever involved in an accident.  It looks FANTASTIC!

While they were working on it, they kept me up-to-date on the car's progress.  In all, they DID have my car for about ten days... but looking at the finished product makes it all worthwhile.  Getting the job done correctly, the first time, is what's most important.  (And in Danny's defense, he was gone on vacation for most of that time, meaning his shop was short-staffed while he was gone.)

I don't have a problem in recommending Big Rig Collision.  I'm very happy with my entire experience with them.  I hope they are still around if I ever need their services again.  - Edward Collins</Text></record>

So first all I would like to give a huge thank you to platinum banquet and their team. I am very happy how everything turned out.
So my sister's quinceanera was this last Saturday. They let us enter the hall at 10 am to prep everything that we needed to do. Like the candy bar the decorations and also the photographer was able to check the dvd player and we had no problems at all. My sister was also able to practice before the actuall dance so that was great.
I met the manger who in charge and he explained everything. Mind you my parents don't speak Spanish so I had to translate. But he explained that 10 mins before they open the buffet they would feed the quinceanera and the crew. Which was so fancy i actually loved it. And we talked about the timing of cutting the cake and the passing for the toast and ECT. He was so helpful. We didn't have plates for the candy bar and he was so nice to give us some. And when I had questions he was always nice about anwsering even if I asked twice. Also the security guard introduce himself and basically explained what his job indicated like the list and If there were to be a problem he would first come to me then if the problem wasn't resolved then he would take furher action. But there was no problems at all. So they were both very helpful and both very nice people. Also the servers were great. Every time I asked for something they would answer and just do what I would ask. Very nice people too. Very please with the management and their team all so helpful with great attitudes.
Now the food was okay. I personally liked it some dishes were good others were not. My family was not a fan. But I think as Latinos were not used to the type of food they provide But like I said they had many options some dishes were great others were not but the food was worth paying for less stress to worry about. Also what banquet halls provide great food. Lmk because I been to many and they all seem the same.  Also they provide chips with salsa, fruits as well. And now for the beer. Overall i was very happy with everything I would definitely recommend this hall to you and my friends to my family.  If you decided to book this hall please book in advance even a year in advance. <user_id>106686682927639163532</user_id>< Text>
Fun place!  Nice setup with a central stage and comfy chairs plus VIP seating as well.  Not a huge venue but just about the right size to sit between cramped and big enough that you need multiple stages (and then have to split attention.)

Couple things to note: this club is FULL nude ... and accordingly a dry 'bar' so no alcohol or byob. $15 cover (they had free-cover cards on the tabled) plus $6 sodas up thru $20 sparking water are available and there's a one-drink minimum.  Dances are topless ($30) or nude ($40)...and couch or bed (+$) and a bit pricey as typical for a full nude club.  What you don't spend on overpriced, watered down drinks they make up on dances.

Monday was pretty quiet but they still had a nice selection of girls which were mostly in their 20s.  All of them were attractive, one or two extremely so (in my opinion at least).  As it was slow, they were a extra friendly and chatty.  Since they don't sell booze all the money comes from dances - so expect a hard sell.  One girl (who's name escapes me) was extremely cute and had some awesome pole dancing tricks too.  I'll miss her!

Security was unobtrusive - no metal detectors or burly bouncers intimidating you for no reason like some other places have. Valet parking is $7 and I didn't notice any street parking nearby. DJ playing a decent mix of music with a number of 90s throwbacks thrown in too.

Overall a great place you should definitely visit if you want dances but since its dry you may want to party elsewhere first.  Since they're open till 4am, you can totally hit them up when the normal bars start shutting down.<//Text>

The biggest jerk ever Manager Wes located the item and blamed me for being upset and wanted me to explain why I was being rude. I explained that Cody told me it was not possible to get my item without paying and I needed it that night. Wes was so condescending and self righteous. He has no understanding that a customer who is told an item is arriving and then is told it is not going to be delivered might be a little stressed and upset.

< review>
If you're concerned with covid I would find an alternative. Three out of four servers assistants wore their mask with their noses exposed both days. When clean plates, water and food were served it was by someone with an exposed face. A cook came out to the restroom with their mask around their chin. Guests waiting were not asked to put on masks nor were guests when using the restroom. Someone forgot their mask and apologized and the young hostess said "it's not a big deal." But all the servers wore their masks correctly and we're very attentive and we're experienced.

No visible management, you could tell they needed help operationally. The front was typically left empty and overwhelmed.

On the other hand, the food was amazing here, five stars for food and one of the reasons I braved it a second visit. Best in Tahoe with reasonable prices and big portions. The outdoor ambiance was very nice as well. You could tell it wasn't thrown together for the pandemic but a long standing portion of the restaurant.</review>

< review>
One of the best Italian restaurant experiences and food I've ever had and well worth the price. We were served warm and soft focaccia bread with oil and vinegar to start. Their Caesar salad was not as creamy as I would have liked, but it was still very tasty. The special for the day, a filet of sole over lemon caper white wine angel hair, was extremely tasty and filling. Their Alfredo sauce has an intricate and layered taste, not just the cheesy goodness in other Italian restaurants. Portions were just right. The tiramisu was lovely. If you're looking for REAL Italian food at a reasonable cost, this is the place!< /review>

<text>Our reservation was for 730 and we arrived sooner than expected. About 45 minutes to be exact. We were took by the host that our tble was being set up. So we waited. There was no bar; however, there was a man playing his saxophone. No bar with a tiny waiting area that could open up to a more comfy, breathable area.

Once we were seated, our waiter came around 10 minutes later to serve us water and champagne. He then came back another 10 minutes later for our appetizer order. The most of the appetizers were delish. We ordered garlic cheese bread, lumaca scusa (escargot), Caesar salad and burrata. I just wish the house butter tasted better for the escargot. It was very bland. And then another 10-15 minutes after our appetizers arrived, the waiter took our entree order.

I ordered the linguine clam. That was a bust! It tasted clammy. Very bland. I even added parmesan cheese, pepper & salt to mask the flavor. I thought it would have more flavor. The clams need to be bathed in some seasoned salt, pepper, garlic, butter, chili powder and some other spices. It tasted as if the clam were taken from its container dumped into the pan with some type of watered down butter sauce and then linguine was added.

I knew I should've played it safe and gone with the spaghetti and meatballs. That is what I would recommend!!! The veal was alright. It could've been better. I should've yelped the place too and read the reviews. A major plus ia that the water refills were on point as well as the upkeep of clearing the empty plates from the table,<//text>< Pics>
